    71	        /// <summary>
    72	        /// Initializes a new instance of ZipArchive on the given stream in the specified mode, specifying whether to leave the stream open.
    73	        /// </summary>
    74	        /// <exception cref="ArgumentException">The stream is already closed. -or- mode is incompatible with the capabilities of the stream.</exception>
    75	        /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException">The stream is null.</exception>
    76	        /// <exception cref="ArgumentOutOfRangeException">mode specified an invalid value.</exception>
    77	        /// <exception cref="InvalidDataException">The contents of the stream could not be interpreted as a Zip file. -or- mode is Update and an entry is missing from the archive or is corrupt and cannot be read. -or- mode is Update and an entry is too large to fit into memory.</exception>
    78	        /// <param name="stream">The input or output stream.</param>
    79	        /// <param name="mode">See the description of the ZipArchiveMode enum. Read requires the stream to support reading, Create requires the stream to support writing, and Update requires the stream to support reading, writing, and seeking.</param>
    80	        /// <param name="leaveOpen">true to leave the stream open upon disposing the ZipArchive, otherwise false.</param>
    81	        /// <param name="entryNameEncoding">The encoding to use when reading or writing entry names and comments in this ZipArchive.
    82	        ///         ///     <para>NOTE: Specifying this parameter to values other than <c>null</c> is discouraged.
    83	        ///         However, this may be necessary for interoperability with ZIP archive tools and libraries that do not correctly support
    84	        ///         UTF-8 encoding for entry names.<br />
    85	        ///         This value is used as follows:</para>
    86	        ///     <para><strong>Reading (opening) ZIP archive files:</strong></para>
    87	        ///     <para>If <c>entryNameEncoding</c> is not specified (<c>== null</c>):</para>
    88	        ///     <list>
    89	        ///         <item>For entries where the language encoding flag (EFS) in the general purpose bit flag of the local file header is <em>not</em> set,
    90	        ///         use the current system default code page (<c>Encoding.Default</c>) in order to decode the entry name and comment.</item>
    91	        ///         <item>For entries where the language encoding flag (EFS) in the general purpose bit flag of the local file header <em>is</em> set,
    92	        ///         use UTF-8 (<c>Encoding.UTF8</c>) in order to decode the entry name and comment.</item>
    93	        ///     </list>
    94	        ///     <para>If <c>entryNameEncoding</c> is specified (<c>!= null</c>):</para>
    95	        ///     <list>
    96	        ///         <item>For entries where the language encoding flag (EFS) in the general purpose bit flag of the local file header is <em>not</em> set,
    97	        ///         use the specified <c>entryNameEncoding</c> in order to decode the entry name and comment.</item>
    98	        ///         <item>For entries where the language encoding flag (EFS) in the general purpose bit flag of the local file header <em>is</em> set,
    99	        ///         use UTF-8 (<c>Encoding.UTF8</c>) in order to decode the entry name and comment.</item>
   100	        ///     </list>
   101	        ///     <para><strong>Writing (saving) ZIP archive files:</strong></para>
   102	        ///     <para>If <c>entryNameEncoding</c> is not specified (<c>== null</c>):</para>
   103	        ///     <list>
   104	        ///         <item>For entry names and comments that contain characters outside the ASCII range,
   105	        ///         the language encoding flag (EFS) will be set in the general purpose bit flag of the local file header,
   106	        ///         and UTF-8 (<c>Encoding.UTF8</c>) will be used in order to encode the entry name and comment into bytes.</item>
   107	        ///         <item>For entry names and comments that do not contain characters outside the ASCII range,
   108	        ///         the language encoding flag (EFS) will not be set in the general purpose bit flag of the local file header,
   109	        ///         and the current system default code page (<c>Encoding.Default</c>) will be used to encode the entry names and comments into bytes.</item>
   110	        ///     </list>
   111	        ///     <para>If <c>entryNameEncoding</c> is specified (<c>!= null</c>):</para>
   112	        ///     <list>
   113	        ///         <item>The specified <c>entryNameEncoding</c> will always be used to encode the entry names and comments into bytes.
   114	        ///         The language encoding flag (EFS) in the general purpose bit flag of the local file header will be set if and only
   115	        ///         if the specified <c>entryNameEncoding</c> is a UTF-8 encoding.</item>
   116	        ///     </list>
   117	        ///     <para>Note that Unicode encodings other than UTF-8 may not be currently used for the <c>entryNameEncoding</c>,
   118	        ///     otherwise an <see cref="ArgumentException"/> is thrown.</para>
   119	        /// </param>
   120	        /// <exception cref="ArgumentException">If a Unicode encoding other than UTF-8 is specified for the <code>entryNameEncoding</code>.</exception>
   121	        public ZipArchive(Stream stream, ZipArchiveMode mode, bool leaveOpen, Encoding? entryNameEncoding)
   122	            : this(mode, leaveOpen, entryNameEncoding, backingStream: null, archiveStream: DecideArchiveStream(mode, stream))
   123	        {
   124	            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(stream);
   125	
   126	            Stream? extraTempStream = null;
   127	
   128	            try
   129	            {
   130	                _backingStream = null;
   131	
   132	                if (ValidateMode(mode, stream))
   133	                {
   134	                    _backingStream = stream;
   135	                    extraTempStream = stream = new MemoryStream();
   136	                    _backingStream.CopyTo(stream);
   137	                    stream.Seek(0, SeekOrigin.Begin);
   138	                }
   139	
   140	                _archiveStream = DecideArchiveStream(mode, stream);
   141	
   142	                switch (mode)
   143	                {
   144	                    case ZipArchiveMode.Create:
   145	                        _readEntries = true;
   146	                        break;
   147	                    case ZipArchiveMode.Read:
   148	                        ReadEndOfCentralDirectory();
   149	                        break;
   150	                    case ZipArchiveMode.Update:
   151	                    default:
   152	                        Debug.Assert(mode == ZipArchiveMode.Update);
   153	                        if (_archiveStream.Length == 0)
   154	                        {
   155	                            _readEntries = true;
   156	                        }
   157	                        else
   158	                        {
   159	                            ReadEndOfCentralDirectory();
   160	                            EnsureCentralDirectoryRead();
   161	
   162	                            foreach (ZipArchiveEntry entry in _entries)
   163	                            {
   164	                                entry.ThrowIfNotOpenable(needToUncompress: false, needToLoadIntoMemory: true);
   165	                            }
   166	                        }
   167	                        break;
   168	                }
   169	            }
   170	            catch (Exception)
   171	            {
   172	                extraTempStream?.Dispose();
   173	
   174	                throw;
   175	            }
   176	        }
   177

   503	        private bool ReadCentralDirectoryEndOfInnerLoopWork(bool result, ZipCentralDirectoryFileHeader? currentHeader, int bytesConsumed, ref bool continueReadingCentralDirectory, ref long numberOfEntries, ref int currPosition, ref int bytesRead)
   504	        {
   505	            if (!result)
   506	            {
   507	                continueReadingCentralDirectory = false;
   508	                return false;
   509	            }
   510	
   511	            Debug.Assert(currentHeader != null, "currentHeader should not be null here");
   512	            AddEntry(new ZipArchiveEntry(this, currentHeader));
   513	            numberOfEntries++;
   514	            if (numberOfEntries > _expectedNumberOfEntries)
   515	            {
   516	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.NumEntriesWrong);
   517	            }
   518	
   519	            currPosition += bytesConsumed;
   520	            bytesRead += bytesConsumed;
   521	
   522	            return true;
   523	        }
   524	
   525	        private void ReadCentralDirectoryEndOfOuterLoopWork(ref int currPosition, ReadOnlySpan<byte> sizedFileBuffer)
   526	        {
   527	            // We've run out of possible space in the entry - seek backwards by the number of bytes remaining in
   528	            // this buffer (so that the next buffer overlaps with this one) and retry.
   529	            if (currPosition < sizedFileBuffer.Length)
   530	            {
   531	                _archiveStream.Seek(-(sizedFileBuffer.Length - currPosition), SeekOrigin.Current);
   532	            }
   533	            currPosition = 0;
   534	        }
   535	
   536	        private void ReadCentralDirectoryPostOuterLoopWork(long numberOfEntries)
   537	        {
   538	            if (numberOfEntries != _expectedNumberOfEntries)
   539	            {
   540	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.NumEntriesWrong);
   541	            }
   542	
   543	            // Sort _entries by each archive entry's position. This supports the algorithm in WriteFile, so is only
   544	            // necessary when the ZipArchive has been opened in Update mode.
   545	            if (Mode == ZipArchiveMode.Update)
   546	            {
   547	                _entries.Sort(ZipArchiveEntry.LocalHeaderOffsetComparer.Instance);
   548	            }
   549	        }
   550	
   551	        private void ReadCentralDirectory()
   552	        {
   553	            try
   554	            {
   555	                ReadCentralDirectoryInitialize(out byte[] fileBuffer, out long numberOfEntries, out bool saveExtraFieldsAndComments, out bool continueReadingCentralDirectory, out int bytesRead, out int currPosition, out int bytesConsumed);
   556	
   557	                Span<byte> fileBufferSpan = fileBuffer.AsSpan();
   558	
   559	                // read the central directory
   560	                while (continueReadingCentralDirectory)
   561	                {
   562	                    // the buffer read must always be large enough to fit the constant section size of at least one header
   563	                    int currBytesRead = _archiveStream.ReadAtLeast(fileBufferSpan, ZipCentralDirectoryFileHeader.BlockConstantSectionSize, throwOnEndOfStream: false);
   564	
   565	                    ReadOnlySpan<byte> sizedFileBuffer = fileBufferSpan.Slice(0, currBytesRead);
   566	                    continueReadingCentralDirectory = currBytesRead >= ZipCentralDirectoryFileHeader.BlockConstantSectionSize;
   567	
   568	                    while (currPosition + ZipCentralDirectoryFileHeader.BlockConstantSectionSize <= currBytesRead)
   569	                    {
   570	                        bool result = ZipCentralDirectoryFileHeader.TryReadBlock(sizedFileBuffer.Slice(currPosition), _archiveStream,
   571	                            saveExtraFieldsAndComments, out bytesConsumed, out ZipCentralDirectoryFileHeader? currentHeader);
   572	
   573	                        if (!ReadCentralDirectoryEndOfInnerLoopWork(result, currentHeader, bytesConsumed, ref continueReadingCentralDirectory, ref numberOfEntries, ref currPosition, ref bytesRead))
   574	                        {
   575	                            break;
   576	                        }
   577	                    }
   578	
   579	                    ReadCentralDirectoryEndOfOuterLoopWork(ref currPosition, sizedFileBuffer);
   580	                }
   581	
   582	                ReadCentralDirectoryPostOuterLoopWork(numberOfEntries);
   583	            }
   584	            catch (EndOfStreamException ex)
   585	            {
   586	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.Format(SR.CentralDirectoryInvalid, ex));
   587	            }
   588	        }
   589	
   590	        private void ReadEndOfCentralDirectoryInnerWork(ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock eocd, out long eocdStart)
   591	        {
   592	            eocdStart = _archiveStream.Position;
   593	
   594	            if (eocd.NumberOfThisDisk != eocd.NumberOfTheDiskWithTheStartOfTheCentralDirectory)
   595	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.SplitSpanned);
   596	
   597	            _numberOfThisDisk = eocd.NumberOfThisDisk;
   598	            _centralDirectoryStart = eocd.OffsetOfStartOfCentralDirectoryWithRespectToTheStartingDiskNumber;
   599	
   600	            if (eocd.NumberOfEntriesInTheCentralDirectory != eocd.NumberOfEntriesInTheCentralDirectoryOnThisDisk)
   601	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.SplitSpanned);
   602	
   603	            _expectedNumberOfEntries = eocd.NumberOfEntriesInTheCentralDirectory;
   604	
   605	            _archiveComment = eocd.ArchiveComment;
   606	        }
   607	
   608	        // This function reads all the EOCD stuff it needs to find the offset to the start of the central directory
   609	        // This offset gets put in _centralDirectoryStart and the number of this disk gets put in _numberOfThisDisk
   610	        // Also does some verification that this isn't a split/spanned archive
   611	        // Also checks that offset to CD isn't out of bounds
   612	        private void ReadEndOfCentralDirectory()
   613	        {
   614	            try
   615	            {
   616	                // This seeks backwards almost to the beginning of the EOCD, one byte after where the signature would be
   617	                // located if the EOCD had the minimum possible size (no file zip comment)
   618	                _archiveStream.Seek(-ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock.SizeOfBlockWithoutSignature, SeekOrigin.End);
   619	
   620	                // If the EOCD has the minimum possible size (no zip file comment), then exactly the previous 4 bytes will contain the signature
   621	                // But if the EOCD has max possible size, the signature should be found somewhere in the previous 64K + 4 bytes
   622	                if (!ZipHelper.SeekBackwardsToSignature(_archiveStream,
   623	                        ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock.SignatureConstantBytes,
   624	                        ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock.ZipFileCommentMaxLength + ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock.FieldLengths.Signature))
   625	                    throw new InvalidDataException(SR.EOCDNotFound);
   626	
   627	                // read the EOCD
   628	                ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock eocd = ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock.ReadBlock(_archiveStream);
   629	
   630	                ReadEndOfCentralDirectoryInnerWork(eocd, out long eocdStart);
   631	
   632	                TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectory(eocd, eocdStart);
   633	
   634	                if (_centralDirectoryStart > _archiveStream.Length)
   635	                {
   636	                    throw new InvalidDataException(SR.FieldTooBigOffsetToCD);
   637	                }
   638	            }
   639	            catch (EndOfStreamException ex)
   640	            {
   641	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt, ex);
   642	            }
   643	            catch (IOException ex)
   644	            {
   645	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt, ex);
   646	            }
   647	        }
   648	
   649	        private void TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectoryInnerInitialWork(Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator? locator)
   650	        {
   651	            if (locator == null || locator.OffsetOfZip64EOCD > long.MaxValue)
   652	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.FieldTooBigOffsetToZip64EOCD);
   653	
   654	            long zip64EOCDOffset = (long)locator.OffsetOfZip64EOCD;
   655	
   656	            _archiveStream.Seek(zip64EOCDOffset, SeekOrigin.Begin);
   657	        }
   658	
   659	        private void TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectoryInnerFinalWork(Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryRecord record)
   660	        {
   661	            _numberOfThisDisk = record.NumberOfThisDisk;
   662	
   663	            if (record.NumberOfEntriesTotal > long.MaxValue)
   664	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.FieldTooBigNumEntries);
   665	
   666	            if (record.OffsetOfCentralDirectory > long.MaxValue)
   667	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.FieldTooBigOffsetToCD);
   668	
   669	            if (record.NumberOfEntriesTotal != record.NumberOfEntriesOnThisDisk)
   670	                throw new InvalidDataException(SR.SplitSpanned);
   671	
   672	            _expectedNumberOfEntries = (long)record.NumberOfEntriesTotal;
   673	            _centralDirectoryStart = (long)record.OffsetOfCentralDirectory;
   674	        }
   675	
   676	        // Tries to find the Zip64 End of Central Directory Locator, then the Zip64 End of Central Directory, assuming the
   677	        // End of Central Directory block has already been found, as well as the location in the stream where the EOCD starts.
   678	        private void TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectory(ZipEndOfCentralDirectoryBlock eocd, long eocdStart)
   679	        {
   680	            // Only bother looking for the Zip64-EOCD stuff if we suspect it is needed because some value is FFFFFFFFF
   681	            // because these are the only two values we need, we only worry about these
   682	            // if we don't find the Zip64-EOCD, we just give up and try to use the original values
   683	            if (eocd.NumberOfThisDisk == ZipHelper.Mask16Bit ||
   684	                eocd.OffsetOfStartOfCentralDirectoryWithRespectToTheStartingDiskNumber == ZipHelper.Mask32Bit ||
   685	                eocd.NumberOfEntriesInTheCentralDirectory == ZipHelper.Mask16Bit)
   686	            {
   687	                // Read Zip64 End of Central Directory Locator
   688	
   689	                // This seeks forwards almost to the beginning of the Zip64-EOCDL, one byte after where the signature would be located
   690	                _archiveStream.Seek(eocdStart - Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.SizeOfBlockWithoutSignature, SeekOrigin.Begin);
   691	
   692	                // Exactly the previous 4 bytes should contain the Zip64-EOCDL signature
   693	                // if we don't find it, assume it doesn't exist and use data from normal EOCD
   694	                if (ZipHelper.SeekBackwardsToSignature(_archiveStream,
   695	                        Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.SignatureConstantBytes,
   696	                        Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.FieldLengths.Signature))
   697	                {
   698	                    // use locator to get to Zip64-EOCD
   699	                    Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator locator = Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlock(_archiveStream);
   700	                    TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectoryInnerInitialWork(locator);

   710	        private static void WriteFileCalculateOffsets(ZipArchiveEntry entry, ref long startingOffset, ref long nextFileOffset)
   711	        {
   712	            if (entry.Changes == ChangeState.Unchanged)
   713	            {
   714	                // Keep track of the expected position of the file entry after the final untouched file entry so that when the loop completes,
   715	                // we'll know which position to start writing new entries from.
   716	                nextFileOffset = Math.Max(nextFileOffset, entry.GetOffsetOfCompressedData() + entry.CompressedLength);
   717	            }
   718	            // When calculating the starting offset to load the files from, only look at changed entries which are already in the archive.
   719	            else
   720	            {
   721	                startingOffset = Math.Min(startingOffset, entry.OffsetOfLocalHeader);
   722	            }
   723	        }
   724	
   725	        private static void WriteFileCheckStartingOffset(ZipArchiveEntry entry, ref long completeRewriteStartingOffset)
   726	        {
   727	            // If the pending data to write is fixed-length metadata in the header, there's no need to load the compressed file bits.
   728	            // We always need to load the local file header's metadata though - at this point, this entry will be written out and we
   729	            // want to make sure that we preserve that metadata.
   730	            if ((entry.Changes & (ChangeState.DynamicLengthMetadata | ChangeState.StoredData)) != 0)
   731	            {
   732	                completeRewriteStartingOffset = Math.Min(completeRewriteStartingOffset, entry.OffsetOfLocalHeader);
   733	            }
   734	        }
   735	
   736	        private void WriteFileUpdateModeFinalWork(long startingOffset, long nextFileOffset)
   737	        {
   738	            // If the offset of entries to write from is still at long.MaxValue, then we know that nothing has been deleted,
   739	            // nothing has been modified - so we just want to move to the end of all remaining files in the archive.
   740	            if (startingOffset == long.MaxValue)
   741	            {
   742	                startingOffset = nextFileOffset;
   743	            }
   744	
   745	            _archiveStream.Seek(startingOffset, SeekOrigin.Begin);
   746	        }

# Let'"'"'s see what the data looks like

# According to the ZIP spec, the Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator has:
# - Signature: 4 bytes (0x50 0x4B 0x06 0x07)
# - Number of disk with start of zip64 EOCD: 4 bytes
# - Relative offset of zip64 EOCD: 8 bytes
# - Total number of disks: 4 bytes
# Total size: 20 bytes

print("\nFirst 20 bytes (should be Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator):")
if len(decoded_data) >= 20:
    first_20 = decoded_data[:20]
    print("Hex:", first_20.hex())
    
    # Check signature
    signature = first_20[:4]
    print("Signature:", signature.hex(), "(expected: 504b0607)")
    
    if signature == b'"'"'PK\x06\x07'"'"':
        print("Signature matches Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator")
        
        # Parse the fields
        num_disk = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', first_20[4:8])[0]
        offset = struct.unpack('"'"'<Q'"'"', first_20[8:16])[0] 
        total_disks = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', first_20[16:20])[0]
        
        print(f"Number of disk with zip64 EOCD: {num_disk}")
        print(f"Offset of zip64 EOCD: {offset}")
        print(f"Total number of disks: {total_disks}")
    else:
        print("Signature does NOT match Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator")
else:
    print("Data is less than 20 bytes")'

The problem is in the `TryReadBlock` method of `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator` (line 443 in `/testbed/src/libraries/System.IO.Compression/src/System/IO/Compression/ZipBlocks.cs`). The code has a `Debug.Assert` that assumes the signature was already verified by `SeekBackwardsToSignature`, but this assumption is incorrect.

Looking at the code flow:
1. `ZipHelper.SeekBackwardsToSignature` searches for the signature and positions the stream at the start of the block
2. `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlock` is called and reads the block
3. The `TryReadBlockCore` method checks if the signature matches
4. If it doesn't match, `zip64eocdLocatorProper` becomes false
5. The `Debug.Assert` fails because it assumes the signature was already verified

The issue is that the `SeekBackwardsToSignature` method might find a false positive signature match, or the data might be corrupted in a way that the signature appears to match but the rest of the data is invalid.

import base64
import struct

# The crash input
base64_data = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="

# Decode from base64
decoded_data = base64.b64decode(base64_data)

print("Decoded data (hex):", decoded_data.hex())
print("Length:", len(decoded_data))

# Analyze the structure
# The data appears to contain multiple ZIP structures

# First 4 bytes: 50 50 4b 05 (0x50504b05)
# This looks like a corrupted signature - should be 50 4b 03 04 for local file header
# or 50 4b 01 02 for central directory header

print("\nAnalyzing the data structure:")
print("First 4 bytes:", decoded_data[:4].hex())

# Check if it contains the Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature (50 4b 06 07)
locator_sig = b'"'"'\x50\x4b\x06\x07'"'"'
if locator_sig in decoded_data:
    idx = decoded_data.index(locator_sig)
    print(f"Found Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature at position {idx}")
    
    # Extract the locator block (20 bytes total)
    if idx + 20 <= len(decoded_data):
        locator_block = decoded_data[idx:idx+20]
        print("Locator block:", locator_block.hex())
        
        # Parse the fields
        num_disk = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', locator_block[4:8])[0]
        offset = struct.unpack('"'"'<Q'"'"', locator_block[8:16])[0] 
        total_disks = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', locator_block[16:20])[0]
        
        print(f"Number of disk with zip64 EOCD: {num_disk}")
        print(f"Offset of zip64 EOCD: {offset}")
        print(f"Total number of disks: {total_disks}")
else:
    print("Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature NOT found")

# Check for other ZIP signatures
signatures = {
    '"'"'Local File Header'"'"': b'"'"'\x50\x4b\x03\x04'"'"',
    '"'"'Central Directory Header'"'"': b'"'"'\x50\x4b\x01\x02'"'"',
    '"'"'End of Central Directory'"'"': b'"'"'\x50\x4b\x05\x06'"'"',
    '"'"'Zip64 End of Central Directory'"'"': b'"'"'\x50\x4b\x06\x06'"'"',
    '"'"'Zip64 End of Central Directory Locator'"'"': b'"'"'\x50\x4b\x06\x07'"'"'
}

print("\nSearching for ZIP signatures:")
for name, sig in signatures.items():
    if sig in decoded_data:
        idx = decoded_data.index(sig)
        print(f"Found {name} signature at position {idx}")'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/analyze_debug.py --file_text '#!/usr/bin/env python3
import base64
import struct

# The crash input
base64_data = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="

decoded_data = base64.b64decode(base64_data)
print("Full data (hex):", decoded_data.hex())
print("Length:", len(decoded_data))

# Analyze byte by byte
print("\nDetailed analysis:")

# Position 0-4: 50 50 4b 05 - corrupted signature?
print("Bytes 0-3:", decoded_data[0:4].hex(), "(looks like corrupted PK.. signature)")

# Position 1-4: 50 4b 05 06 - End of Central Directory signature
print("Bytes 1-4:", decoded_data[1:5].hex(), "- End of Central Directory signature (50 4b 05 06)")

# End of Central Directory block should be 22 bytes
# Signature (4) + disk numbers (2+2) + entry counts (2+2) + CD size (4) + CD offset (4) + comment length (2)
eocd_start = 1
eocd_end = eocd_start + 22

if len(decoded_data) >= eocd_end:
    eocd_block = decoded_data[eocd_start:eocd_end]
    print("\nEnd of Central Directory block:", eocd_block.hex())
    
    # Parse EOCD fields
    disk_num = struct.unpack('"'"'<H'"'"', eocd_block[4:6])[0]
    cd_disk = struct.unpack('"'"'<H'"'"', eocd_block[6:8])[0]
    disk_entries = struct.unpack('"'"'<H'"'"', eocd_block[8:10])[0]
    total_entries = struct.unpack('"'"'<H'"'"', eocd_block[10:12])[0]
    cd_size = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', eocd_block[12:16])[0]
    cd_offset = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', eocd_block[16:20])[0]
    comment_len = struct.unpack('"'"'<H'"'"', eocd_block[20:22])[0]
    
    print(f"Disk number: {disk_num}")
    print(f"CD disk: {cd_disk}") 
    print(f"Disk entries: {disk_entries}")
    print(f"Total entries: {total_entries}")
    print(f"CD size: {cd_size}")
    print(f"CD offset: {cd_offset}")
    print(f"Comment length: {comment_len}")
    
    # Check for ZIP64 indicators
    if disk_num == 0xFFFF or cd_offset == 0xFFFFFFFF or total_entries == 0xFFFF:
        print("\nZIP64 indicators detected!")
        
# Position 25-29: 50 4b 06 07 - Zip64 End of Central Directory Locator
locator_start = 25
locator_end = locator_start + 20

if len(decoded_data) >= locator_end:
    locator_block = decoded_data[locator_start:locator_end]
    print("\nZip64 End of Central Directory Locator:", locator_block.hex())
    
    num_disk = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', locator_block[4:8])[0]
    offset = struct.unpack('"'"'<Q'"'"', locator_block[8:16])[0] 
    total_disks = struct.unpack('"'"'<I'"'"', locator_block[16:20])[0]
    
    print(f"Number of disk with zip64 EOCD: {num_disk}")
    print(f"Offset of zip64 EOCD: {offset}")
    print(f"Total number of disks: {total_disks}")
    
    # The issue: The Zip64 locator points to an offset, but there'"'"'s no Zip64 EOCD record!
    print("\nPROBLEM: Zip64 locator exists but points to offset", offset)
    print("There'"'"'s no Zip64 EOCD record at that position in the data!")
    
# Let'"'"'s see what the algorithm does:
# 1. It finds EOCD at position 1
# 2. Sees ZIP64 indicators (probably cd_offset = 0xFFFFFFFF)
# 3. Seeks backwards to find Zip64 locator signature
# 4. Finds locator at position 25
# 5. Tries to read the locator block
# 6. Uses the offset from locator to seek to Zip64 EOCD
# 7. But there'"'"'s no data there!

print("\n=== The Bug Scenario ===")
print("1. EOCD found with ZIP64 indicators")
print("2. Zip64 locator found at position 25") 
print("3. Locator points to Zip64 EOCD at offset", offset)
print("4. But stream position after reading locator is:", locator_end)
print("5. Seeking to offset", offset, "would go to:", offset)
print("6. But data ends at position", len(decoded_data))
print("7. There'"'"'s no Zip64 EOCD record at offset", offset)'

The problematic line is:
```csharp
Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null);
```

The comment says "we just found this using the signature finder, so it should be okay", but this assumption is flawed. The signature finder might find a signature somewhere in the data, but when we try to read the full block, there might not be enough bytes remaining in the stream to read the entire block.

In the fuzzing case:
1. The signature finder finds `50 4b 06 07` at position 25
2. It positions the stream at the beginning of the signature
3. `TryReadBlock` tries to read 20 bytes
4. But there are only 12 bytes left (37 total - 25 position = 12 bytes remaining)
5. `ReadAtLeast` returns only 12 bytes, so `bytesRead < TotalSize` (12 < 20)
6. `TryReadBlockCore` returns false
7. But the assertion assumes it should succeed

Let me check the exact behavior

if remaining_bytes >= 20:
    full_block = decoded_data[locator_pos:locator_pos+20]
    print("Full block:", full_block.hex())
else:
    partial_block = decoded_data[locator_pos:]
    print("Partial block (only", len(partial_block), "bytes available):", partial_block.hex())'

Perfect! Now I've confirmed the exact issue. The problem is that the assertion in `Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlock` is wrong. It assumes that if we found the signature, we must be able to read the full block. However, in this case:

1. There are only 37 bytes total
2. The signature is found at position 25
3. Only 12 bytes remain (37 - 25 = 12)
4. The locator block needs 20 bytes
5. `ReadAtLeast` reads only 12 bytes (what's available)
6. `TryReadBlockCore` returns false because `bytesRead < TotalSize` (12 < 20)
7. But the assertion expects success

The fix is simple: instead of having a debug assertion that might fail, we should handle the case where `TryReadBlockCore` returns false by throwing an appropriate exception or returning null.

Let me look at how other similar methods handle this:

        // The crash input

        {
            using var stream = new MemoryStream(data);
            using var archive = new ZipArchive(stream, ZipArchiveMode.Read);

            Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: ZipArchive created without assertion failure!");
            Console.WriteLine("Number of entries: " + archive.Entries.Count);

Verifying the fix for the ZipArchive assertion failure...

Found TryReadBlock method. Checking the implementation...

✓ FIX APPLIED: The method now throws InvalidDataException when TryReadBlockCore returns false
✓ GOOD: The problematic Debug.Assert has been removed

Current implementation of TryReadBlock:
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 1: public static Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator TryReadBlock(Stream stream)
 2:         {
 3:             Span<byte> blockContents = stackalloc byte[TotalSize];
 4:             int bytesRead = stream.ReadAtLeast(blockContents, blockContents.Length, throwOnEndOfStream: false);
 5:             bool zip64eocdLocatorProper = TryReadBlockCore(blockContents, bytesRead, out Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator? zip64EOCDLocator);
 6: 
 7:             // If we found the signature but couldn't read the complete block, throw an appropriate exception
 8:             if (!zip64eocdLocatorProper)
 9:             {
10:                 throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt);
11:             }
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

=== Fix Summary ===
The fix changes the behavior from:
  - Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null)
  - return zip64EOCDLocator; // could be null!

To:
  - if (!zip64eocdLocatorProper) throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt);
  - Debug.Assert(zip64EOCDLocator != null); // now this is safe
  - return zip64EOCDLocator;

This ensures that corrupt data (where signature is found but not enough bytes
are available to read the full block) throws a proper exception instead of
causing an assertion failure.

import base64

print("Testing edge cases for the ZipArchive fix...\n")

# Edge case 1: Original crash case - locator signature found but not enough bytes
print("=== Edge Case 1: Original Crash Case ===")

print(f"Has locator signature: {b'"'"'PK\\x06\\x07'"'"' in decoded_data1}")
print(f"Bytes after signature: {len(decoded_data1) - decoded_data1.index(b'"'"'PK\\x06\\x07'"'"')}")
print("Expected behavior: Should throw InvalidDataException\n")

# Edge case 2: Complete locator block but no Zip64 EOCD record
print("=== Edge Case 2: Complete Locator but No Zip64 EOCD ===")

# The fix handles this through the existing logic in TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectory
print("Expected behavior: Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryRecord.TryReadBlock should throw\n")

# Edge case 3: No locator signature at all
print("=== Edge Case 3: No Locator Signature ===")
# If no locator signature is found, the code should fall back to using regular EOCD data

+using System;
+using System.IO;
+using System.IO.Compression;
+
+class TestZipArchiveFix
+{
+    static void Main()
+    {
+        // The crash input
+        string base64Data = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ==";
+        byte[] data = Convert.FromBase64String(base64Data);
+        
+        Console.WriteLine("Testing ZipArchive with fuzzer crash input...");
+        Console.WriteLine("Data length: " + data.Length);
+        
+        try
+        {
+            using var stream = new MemoryStream(data);
+            using var archive = new ZipArchive(stream, ZipArchiveMode.Read);
+            
+            // If we get here without an exception, the fix worked
+            Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: ZipArchive created without assertion failure!");
+            Console.WriteLine("Number of entries: " + archive.Entries.Count);
+        }
+        catch (InvalidDataException ex)
+        {
+            // This is expected - the data is corrupt, so it should throw InvalidDataException
+            Console.WriteLine("SUCCESS: InvalidDataException thrown (as expected for corrupt data): " + ex.Message);
+        }
+        catch (Exception ex)
+        {
+            // Any other exception suggests the fix didn't work properly
+            Console.WriteLine("UNEXPECTED EXCEPTION: " + ex.GetType().Name + ": " + ex.Message);
+            if (ex.InnerException != null)
+            {
+                Console.WriteLine("Inner Exception: " + ex.InnerException.GetType().Name + ": " + ex.InnerException.Message);
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import base64
+import struct
+
+# The crash input
+base64_data = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="
+
+decoded_data = base64.b64decode(base64_data)
+print("Full data (hex):", decoded_data.hex())
+print("Length:", len(decoded_data))
+
+# Analyze byte by byte
+print("\nDetailed analysis:")
+
+# Position 0-4: 50 50 4b 05 - corrupted signature?
+print("Bytes 0-3:", decoded_data[0:4].hex(), "(looks like corrupted PK.. signature)")
+
+# Position 1-4: 50 4b 05 06 - End of Central Directory signature
+print("Bytes 1-4:", decoded_data[1:5].hex(), "- End of Central Directory signature (50 4b 05 06)")
+
+# End of Central Directory block should be 22 bytes
+# Signature (4) + disk numbers (2+2) + entry counts (2+2) + CD size (4) + CD offset (4) + comment length (2)
+eocd_start = 1
+eocd_end = eocd_start + 22
+
+if len(decoded_data) >= eocd_end:
+    eocd_block = decoded_data[eocd_start:eocd_end]
+    print("\nEnd of Central Directory block:", eocd_block.hex())
+    
+    # Parse EOCD fields
+    disk_num = struct.unpack('<H', eocd_block[4:6])[0]
+    cd_disk = struct.unpack('<H', eocd_block[6:8])[0]
+    disk_entries = struct.unpack('<H', eocd_block[8:10])[0]
+    total_entries = struct.unpack('<H', eocd_block[10:12])[0]
+    cd_size = struct.unpack('<I', eocd_block[12:16])[0]
+    cd_offset = struct.unpack('<I', eocd_block[16:20])[0]
+    comment_len = struct.unpack('<H', eocd_block[20:22])[0]
+    
+    print(f"Disk number: {disk_num}")
+    print(f"CD disk: {cd_disk}") 
+    print(f"Disk entries: {disk_entries}")
+    print(f"Total entries: {total_entries}")
+    print(f"CD size: {cd_size}")
+    print(f"CD offset: {cd_offset}")
+    print(f"Comment length: {comment_len}")
+    
+    # Check for ZIP64 indicators
+    if disk_num == 0xFFFF or cd_offset == 0xFFFFFFFF or total_entries == 0xFFFF:
+        print("\nZIP64 indicators detected!")
+        
+# Position 25-29: 50 4b 06 07 - Zip64 End of Central Directory Locator
+locator_start = 25
+locator_end = locator_start + 20
+
+offset = 0  # Initialize variable
+
+if len(decoded_data) >= locator_end:
+    locator_block = decoded_data[locator_start:locator_end]
+    print("\nZip64 End of Central Directory Locator:", locator_block.hex())
+    
+    num_disk = struct.unpack('<I', locator_block[4:8])[0]
+    offset = struct.unpack('<Q', locator_block[8:16])[0] 
+    total_disks = struct.unpack('<I', locator_block[16:20])[0]
+    
+    print(f"Number of disk with zip64 EOCD: {num_disk}")
+    print(f"Offset of zip64 EOCD: {offset}")
+    print(f"Total number of disks: {total_disks}")
+    
+    # The issue: The Zip64 locator points to an offset, but there's no Zip64 EOCD record!
+    print("\nPROBLEM: Zip64 locator exists but points to offset", offset)
+    print("There's no Zip64 EOCD record at that position in the data!")
+    
+# Let's see what the algorithm does:
+# 1. It finds EOCD at position 1
+# 2. Sees ZIP64 indicators (probably cd_offset = 0xFFFFFFFF)
+# 3. Seeks backwards to find Zip64 locator signature
+# 4. Finds locator at position 25
+# 5. Tries to read the locator block
+# 6. Uses the offset from locator to seek to Zip64 EOCD
+# 7. But there's no data there!
+
+print("\n=== The Bug Scenario ===")
+print("1. EOCD found with ZIP64 indicators")
+print("2. Zip64 locator found at position 25") 
+print("3. Locator points to Zip64 EOCD at offset", offset)
+print("4. But stream position after reading locator is:", locator_end)
+print("5. Seeking to offset", offset, "would go to:", offset)
+print("6. But data ends at position", len(decoded_data))
+print("7. There's no Zip64 EOCD record at offset", offset)

+import base64
+import struct
+
+# The crash input
+base64_data = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="
+
+# Decode from base64
+decoded_data = base64.b64decode(base64_data)
+
+print("Decoded data (hex):", decoded_data.hex())
+print("Length:", len(decoded_data))
+
+# Try to parse the data as a ZIP structure
+# The crash is happening in Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.TryReadBlock
+# Let's see what the data looks like
+
+# According to the ZIP spec, the Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator has:
+# - Signature: 4 bytes (0x50 0x4B 0x06 0x07)
+# - Number of disk with start of zip64 EOCD: 4 bytes
+# - Relative offset of zip64 EOCD: 8 bytes
+# - Total number of disks: 4 bytes
+# Total size: 20 bytes
+
+print("\nFirst 20 bytes (should be Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator):")
+if len(decoded_data) >= 20:
+    first_20 = decoded_data[:20]
+    print("Hex:", first_20.hex())
+    
+    # Check signature
+    signature = first_20[:4]
+    print("Signature:", signature.hex(), "(expected: 504b0607)")
+    
+    if signature == b'PK\x06\x07':
+        print("Signature matches Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator")
+        
+        # Parse the fields
+        num_disk = struct.unpack('<I', first_20[4:8])[0]
+        offset = struct.unpack('<Q', first_20[8:16])[0] 
+        total_disks = struct.unpack('<I', first_20[16:20])[0]
+        
+        print(f"Number of disk with zip64 EOCD: {num_disk}")
+        print(f"Offset of zip64 EOCD: {offset}")
+        print(f"Total number of disks: {total_disks}")
+    else:
+        print("Signature does NOT match Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator")
+else:
+    print("Data is less than 20 bytes")

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import os
+
+print("=== Final Verification of the ZipArchive Fix ===\n")
+
+# Verify both synchronous and asynchronous versions were fixed
+files_to_check = [
+    "/testbed/src/libraries/System.IO.Compression/src/System/IO/Compression/ZipBlocks.cs",
+    "/testbed/src/libraries/System.IO.Compression/src/System/IO/Compression/ZipBlocks.Async.cs"
+]
+
+fix_applied = True
+
+for file_path in files_to_check:
+    print(f"Checking: {os.path.basename(file_path)}")
+    
+    if not os.path.exists(file_path):
+        print("  ✗ File not found")
+        fix_applied = False
+        continue
+        
+    with open(file_path, 'r') as f:
+        content = f.read()
+    
+    # Check for the synchronous TryReadBlock method
+    if "TryReadBlock(Stream stream)" in content:
+        method_start = content.find("public static Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator TryReadBlock(Stream stream)")
+        method_end = content.find("}", method_start)
+        method_content = content[method_start:method_end+1]
+        
+        has_proper_check = "if (!zip64eocdLocatorProper)" in method_content and "throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt)" in method_content
+        has_problematic_assert = "Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null)" in method_content
+        
+        if has_proper_check and not has_problematic_assert:
+            print("  ✓ Synchronous TryReadBlock method properly fixed")
+        else:
+            print("  ✗ Synchronous TryReadBlock method not properly fixed")
+            fix_applied = False
+    
+    # Check for the asynchronous TryReadBlockAsync method  
+    if "TryReadBlockAsync" in content:
+        async_start = content.find("public static async Task<Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator> TryReadBlockAsync")
+        async_end = content.find("}", async_start)
+        async_content = content[async_start:async_end+1]
+        
+        has_async_check = "if (!zip64eocdLocatorProper)" in async_content and "throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt)" in async_content
+        has_async_problem = "Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null)" in async_content
+        
+        if has_async_check and not has_async_problem:
+            print("  ✓ Asynchronous TryReadBlockAsync method properly fixed")
+        else:
+            print("  ✗ Asynchronous TryReadBlockAsync method not properly fixed")
+            fix_applied = False
+
+print("\n" + "="*60)
+
+if fix_applied:
+    print("SUCCESS: The fix has been properly applied to both synchronous and")
+    print("         asynchronous implementations of Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator.")
+    print("\nThe fix ensures that when corrupt ZIP data is encountered (where the")
+    print("Zip64 locator signature is found but there's not enough data to read")
+    print("the complete block), it throws a proper InvalidDataException instead")
+    print("of causing an assertion failure.")
+else:
+    print("ERROR: The fix was not properly applied to all required methods.")
+
+print("\n=== Issue Details ===")
+print("Original Problem: Debug.Assert failed when corrupt ZIP data was processed")
+print("Root Cause: Signature found but not enough bytes available to read full block")
+print("Fix: Replace Debug.Assert with proper exception handling")
+print("Result: Graceful error handling instead of crashes")

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import base64
+
+# The crash input
+base64_data = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="
+decoded_data = base64.b64decode(base64_data)
+
+print("Data length:", len(decoded_data))
+print("Data (hex):", decoded_data.hex())
+
+# Position of Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature
+locator_pos = 25
+print("\nZip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature at position:", locator_pos)
+print("Bytes at position 25:", decoded_data[locator_pos:locator_pos+4].hex())
+
+# Bytes remaining after positioning at signature
+remaining_bytes = len(decoded_data) - locator_pos
+print("Bytes remaining after position 25:", remaining_bytes)
+
+# Total size of Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator block
+locator_total_size = 20  # 4 bytes signature + 16 bytes data
+print("Total size needed for Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator:", locator_total_size)
+
+print("\nPROBLEM: Only", remaining_bytes, "bytes available, but need", locator_total_size, "bytes!")
+print("This is why TryReadBlockCore returns false!")
+
+# Let's see what actually happens when we try to read the remaining bytes
+if remaining_bytes >= 4:
+    print("\nFirst 4 bytes (signature):", decoded_data[locator_pos:locator_pos+4].hex())
+if remaining_bytes >= 20:
+    full_block = decoded_data[locator_pos:locator_pos+20]
+    print("Full block:", full_block.hex())
+else:
+    partial_block = decoded_data[locator_pos:]
+    print("Partial block (only", len(partial_block), "bytes available):", partial_block.hex())

+# Edge case 1: Original crash case - locator signature found but not enough bytes
+print("=== Edge Case 1: Original Crash Case ===")
+base64_data1 = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="
+decoded_data1 = base64.b64decode(base64_data1)
+print(f"Length: {len(decoded_data1)}")
+print(f"Has locator signature: {b'PK\\x06\\x07' in decoded_data1}")
+print(f"Bytes after signature: {len(decoded_data1) - decoded_data1.index(b'PK\\x06\\x07')}")
+print("Expected behavior: Should throw InvalidDataException\n")
+
+# Edge case 2: Complete locator block but no Zip64 EOCD record
+print("=== Edge Case 2: Complete Locator but No Zip64 EOCD ===")
+# This would require creating a test case with a complete locator block but no record.
+# The fix handles this through the existing logic in TryReadZip64EndOfCentralDirectory
+print("Expected behavior: Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryRecord.TryReadBlock should throw\n")
+
+# Edge case 3: No locator signature at all
+print("=== Edge Case 3: No Locator Signature ===")
+# If no locator signature is found, the code should fall back to using regular EOCD data
+print("Expected behavior: Use regular EOCD data (no ZIP64 indicators)\n")
+
+# Edge case 4: Corrupted locator data
+print("=== Edge Case 4: Corrupted Locator Data ===")
+# If the locator data is corrupted (e.g., invalid offset), existing validation should handle it
+print("Expected behavior: Throw appropriate exception based on existing validation\n")
+
+print("=== Summary of the Fix ===")
+print("The fix addresses the specific case where:")
+print("1. ZIP64 indicators are found in EOCD")
+print("2. Zip64 locator signature is found")
+print("3. But there aren't enough bytes to read the complete locator block")
+print("")
+print("Previously: Debug.Assert would fail in release builds, causing crashes")
+print("Now: InvalidDataException is thrown, allowing graceful error handling")
+print("")
+print("This fix is minimal and focused on the specific assertion failure issue.")
+print("It preserves all existing validation for other edge cases.")

@@ -0,0 +1,59 @@
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import base64
+import struct
+
+# The crash input
+base64_data = "UFBLBQYAAAAA//////9YaQRhAAAAAAAAAFBLBgcAAEsFBv//BQ=="
+
+# Decode from base64
+decoded_data = base64.b64decode(base64_data)
+
+print("Decoded data (hex):", decoded_data.hex())
+print("Length:", len(decoded_data))
+
+# Analyze the structure
+# The data appears to contain multiple ZIP structures
+
+# First 4 bytes: 50 50 4b 05 (0x50504b05)
+# This looks like a corrupted signature - should be 50 4b 03 04 for local file header
+# or 50 4b 01 02 for central directory header
+
+print("\nAnalyzing the data structure:")
+print("First 4 bytes:", decoded_data[:4].hex())
+
+# Check if it contains the Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature (50 4b 06 07)
+locator_sig = b'\x50\x4b\x06\x07'
+if locator_sig in decoded_data:
+    idx = decoded_data.index(locator_sig)
+    print(f"Found Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature at position {idx}")
+    
+    # Extract the locator block (20 bytes total)
+    if idx + 20 <= len(decoded_data):
+        locator_block = decoded_data[idx:idx+20]
+        print("Locator block:", locator_block.hex())
+        
+        # Parse the fields
+        num_disk = struct.unpack('<I', locator_block[4:8])[0]
+        offset = struct.unpack('<Q', locator_block[8:16])[0] 
+        total_disks = struct.unpack('<I', locator_block[16:20])[0]
+        
+        print(f"Number of disk with zip64 EOCD: {num_disk}")
+        print(f"Offset of zip64 EOCD: {offset}")
+        print(f"Total number of disks: {total_disks}")
+else:
+    print("Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator signature NOT found")
+
+# Check for other ZIP signatures
+signatures = {
+    'Local File Header': b'\x50\x4b\x03\x04',
+    'Central Directory Header': b'\x50\x4b\x01\x02',
+    'End of Central Directory': b'\x50\x4b\x05\x06',
+    'Zip64 End of Central Directory': b'\x50\x4b\x06\x06',
+    'Zip64 End of Central Directory Locator': b'\x50\x4b\x06\x07'
+}
+
+print("\nSearching for ZIP signatures:")
+for name, sig in signatures.items():
+    if sig in decoded_data:
+        idx = decoded_data.index(sig)
+        print(f"Found {name} signature at position {idx}")

+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import os
+
+# Verify that the fix has been applied correctly
+zip_blocks_path = "/testbed/src/libraries/System.IO.Compression/src/System/IO/Compression/ZipBlocks.cs"
+
+print("Verifying the fix for the ZipArchive assertion failure...\n")
+
+# Check that the file exists
+if not os.path.exists(zip_blocks_path):
+    print("ERROR: File not found:", zip_blocks_path)
+    exit(1)
+
+with open(zip_blocks_path, 'r') as f:
+    content = f.read()
+
+# Look for the TryReadBlock method in Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator
+locator_start = content.find("public static Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator TryReadBlock(Stream stream)")
+if locator_start == -1:
+    print("ERROR: Could not find TryReadBlock method in Zip64EndOfCentralDirectoryLocator")
+    exit(1)
+
+# Extract the method
+method_end = content.find("}", locator_start)
+if method_end == -1:
+    method_end = len(content)
+
+method_content = content[locator_start:method_end+1]
+
+print("Found TryReadBlock method. Checking the implementation...\n")
+
+# Check if the fix has been applied
+if "throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt);" in method_content:
+    print("✓ FIX APPLIED: The method now throws InvalidDataException when TryReadBlockCore returns false")
+else:
+    print("✗ FIX NOT APPLIED: The method still has the problematic Debug.Assert")
+    
+# Check that the problematic Debug.Assert is not present
+if "Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null)" in method_content:
+    print("✗ PROBLEM: The problematic Debug.Assert is still present")
+else:
+    print("✓ GOOD: The problematic Debug.Assert has been removed")
+
+# Show the current implementation
+print("\nCurrent implementation of TryReadBlock:")
+print("-" * 80)
+lines = method_content.split('\n')
+for i, line in enumerate(lines):
+    print(f"{i+1:2}: {line}")
+print("-" * 80)
+
+print("\n=== Fix Summary ===")
+print("The fix changes the behavior from:")
+print("  - Debug.Assert(zip64eocdLocatorProper && zip64EOCDLocator != null)")
+print("  - return zip64EOCDLocator; // could be null!")
+print("")
+print("To:")
+print("  - if (!zip64eocdLocatorProper) throw new InvalidDataException(SR.CDCorrupt);")
+print("  - Debug.Assert(zip64EOCDLocator != null); // now this is safe")
+print("  - return zip64EOCDLocator;")
+print("")
+print("This ensures that corrupt data (where signature is found but not enough bytes")
+print("are available to read the full block) throws a proper exception instead of")
+print("causing an assertion failure.")
